#Inauguration Speech
country_event = {
	id = LBJ.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.1"}
	title = LBJ.1.t
	desc = LBJ.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = LBJ.1.a
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

#Flavor event about drafting up plans and deteriming what the GS will be about
country_event = {
	id = LBJ.11
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.11"}
	title = LBJ.11.t
	desc = LBJ.11.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_congress2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Lets do this thing
		name = LBJ.11.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_strengthen_republicans_party
		add_political_power = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = { #Influence boost for your wing of the party
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { RD_popularity > NPP_popularity }
					NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchanging corn
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.04 }
			}
		}
	}
}

					limit = {

					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.03 }

			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_LBJ_increase_NPP_demand_urgency_tt
		add_to_variable = { LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand = 1 }

			limit = {
				can_have_elections_in_state = yes
				check_variable = { NPP_popularity > RD_popularity }

				NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchanging Corn
			}
			add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.04}
			add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 85 } }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.025 }
			}
		}
	}

#Wallace celebrates--he's still got it
country_event = {
	id = LBJ.19
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.19"}
	title = LBJ.19.t
	desc = LBJ.19.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #oops
		name = LBJ.19.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_LBJ_racism_gonna_racism
		subtract_from_variable = { LBJ_civil_rights_strength = 5 }
		subtract_from_variable = { tno_minorities_effectiveness = 5 }
		TNO_update_minorities_policy_effectiveness = yes
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				can_have_elections_in_state = yes
				OR = {
					check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
					check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
					check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.06 }
			if = { #Bigger gains for them in Dixie
				limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 83 } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = LBJ.20 days = 7 } }
	}
}

					limit = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { RD_popularity < NPP_popularity } }
						add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }
					}
					else = { add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 } }
				}
				US_underdog_RD_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

					}

						limit = { check_variable = { RD_popularity < NPP_popularity }}
						add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }
					}
					else = { add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Determining how strong to make the immigration bill
country_event = {
	id = LBJ.60
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.60"}
	title = LBJ.60.t
	desc = LBJ.60.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				60 = { country_event = { id = LBJ.61 days = 21 } } #Hans made his way to America
				40 = {} #Hans dies on the way to his homeplanet or something i guess
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #strong
		name = LBJ.60.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_nativist_backlash
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = LBJ_immigration_strong
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchanging Corn
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { RD_popularity > NPP_popularity }
							check_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity > RD_R_bonus_popularity }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { NPP_popularity > RD_popularity }
							check_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity > NPP_C_bonus_popularity }
						}
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.07 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = 0.02 } #Fucking fascists
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #weak
		name = LBJ.60.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_nativist_progressive_backlash
		add_political_power = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = LBJ_immigration_weak
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchanging Corn
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { RD_popularity > NPP_popularity }
							check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity > RD_D_bonus_popularity }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { NPP_popularity > RD_popularity }
							check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
						}
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.07 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = 0.02 } #Internationale intensifies unpog
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}

				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = -0.03}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = -0.03}
				if = { #UNDERDOG BONUS, PRO NPP
					limit = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 85}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity }}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.025 }
						else = { add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.025 }}
					}
				}
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes

						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee

					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				if = { #Bigger gains for them in New England

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }

			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = LBJ.90
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.90"}
	title = LBJ.90.t
	desc = LBJ.90.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rd_generic1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #yes funding
		name = LBJ.90.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_decrease_southern_popularity
		add_political_power = -40
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
							check_variable = { nationality = 337 } #Unchanging Corn
							AND = { #Support in African American states if LBJ completed his civil rights reforms
								check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
								USA = { has_country_flag = LBJ_completed_civil_rights_reforms }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.06 }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 83 } } #Dixie
					add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = LBJ_Education2_schools_funded
		}
	}
	option = { #no funding
		name = LBJ.90.b
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = LBJ_Education2_schools_not_funded }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

 	#Fine

		custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_strengthen_democrats_party
		custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_center_cannibalize
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 2.25 }
			clr_country_flag = USA_R_Center_United
			country_event = { id = LBJ.95 days = 3 }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity < RD_R_bonus_popularity }
					NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchanging Corn
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.06 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.06 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.04 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.02 }
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#God no why
	option = {
		name = LBJ.94.b
		add_political_power = -75
		subtract_from_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 2.5 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_subtract_RD_unity
	}
}

							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee

							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}
					}

				}

					subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.03 }
					add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.03 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.02 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.02 }
				}
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}

	title = LBJ.104.t
	desc = LBJ.104.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rd_generic2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = LBJ.104.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_exhuastion_tt_med
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchanging corn
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.06 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.06 } #Less enthusiaism
					add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.03 } #Conservative shift
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.03 }
				}
				else = {
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.06 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.06 }
					add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.06 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
				}
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#7 - Big migration of progressives from RD to NPP-C
country_event = {
	id = LBJ.106
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.106"}
	title = LBJ.106.t
	desc = LBJ.106.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rd_generic3

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = LBJ.106.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_exhuastion_tt_high
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
				}

				set_temp_variable = {RD_total_pop = RD_R_bonus_popularity}
				add_to_temp_variable = { RD_total_pop = RD_D_bonus_popularity} #RD pop summed

				set_temp_variable = { NPP_total_pop = NPP_C_bonus_popularity}
				add_to_temp_variable = { NPP_total_pop = NPP_FR_bonus_popularity}
				add_to_temp_variable = { NPP_total_pop = NPP_Y_bonus_popularity}
				add_to_temp_variable = { NPP_total_pop = NPP_L_bonus_popularity} #NPP pop summed

				set_temp_variable = { R_temp = RD_R_bonus_popularity}
				divide_temp_variable = {R_temp = 3} #1/3 of Republican strength

				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = R_temp}  #leave the party...

				divide_temp_variable = {R_temp = RD_total_pop} #Proportion of the party strength coming from these 30% republicans

				multiply_temp_variable = {R_temp = RD_popularity} #Amount of the party strength coming from these 30% republicans

				subtract_from_variable = {RD_popularity = R_temp } #leave the party..
				add_to_variable = {NPP_popularity = R_temp} #...to the NPP

				divide_temp_variable = {R_temp = NPP_popularity }
				multiply_temp_variable = {R_temp = NPP_total_pop}

				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = R_temp} #... Center

				US_underdog_NPP_5_5 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

			add_to_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = -0.75 }

				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { senator_1 = 2}
				}
				set_variable = { senator_1 = 6}
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = -0.1 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.05}

					limit = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 85}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity }}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
					}
					else = {
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.025 }
					}
				}
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}

				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { senator_2 = 2}
				}
				set_variable = { senator_2 = 6}

				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.05}

					}

						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.025 }
					}
				}
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}

			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { senator_2 = 2}
				}
				set_variable = { senator_2 = 6}

				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}

country_event = {
	id = LBJ.126
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LBJ.126"}
	title = LBJ.126.t
	desc = LBJ.126.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_presidential_podium

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #income
		name = LBJ.126.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_LBJ_income_tax_increase
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NPP_popularity_grows_low
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { income_tax_rate = 0.03 }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchanging Corn
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				if = { #Signifcantly less pushback in North
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
							AND = { #Support in African American states if LBJ has completed his civil rights reforms
								check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
								USA = { has_country_flag = LBJ_completed_civil_rights_reforms }
							}
						}
					}
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_RD_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = LBJ_increase_income_taxes
	}

	option = { #general
		name = LBJ.126.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_LBJ_general_tax_increase
		add_political_power = -75
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NPP_popularity_grows
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { income_tax_rate = 0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { business_tax_rate = 0.03 }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchanging Corn
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.06 }
				if = { #Slightly less pushback in North
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
							AND = { #Support in African American states if LBJ has completed his civil rights reforms
								check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
								USA = { has_country_flag = LBJ_completed_civil_rights_reforms }
							}
						}
					}
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
		}

	}

						subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 } #Let's not hit the NPP too hard
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					US_underdog_RD_2_2 = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = { #Rest of the country is less than pleased
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
								check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
								check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
							}
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.09 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else = { #FULL PROGRESS AHEAD
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_increase_heartland_popularity
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_decrease_southern_popularity_west
			TNO_improve_political_parties_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_state = { #Enjoy the support
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.09 }
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					US_underdog_RD_2_2 = yes
					if = { #Midwest becomes less progressive compared to New England
						limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 85 } }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 } #Let's not hit the NPP too hard
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				}
				every_owned_state = { #Rest of the country is less than pleased
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
								check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							}
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.09 }
					if = { #West Coast is not as angry as the others
						limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 88 } }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
				}
			}
		}
		tno_pensions_improve = yes
		if = { #Apply the extra effects for more reforms
			limit = { has_country_flag = GLN_pension_additional_pensions }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea = tno_unemployment_generous_subsidies } }
					tno_pensions_improve = yes
					set_variable = { tno_pensions_effectiveness = 40 }
					add_to_variable = { USA_GLN_Public_Support = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GLN_pension_anti_poverty }
			TNO_improve_poverty_med = yes
			set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.2 }
			econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
			set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.4 }
			econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { USA_GLN_Public_Support = 5 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = USA_GLN_Public_Support
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
			USA_bill_clear = yes
		}
	}
}

					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 87 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.5 } #Let's not totally ruin any chance the RDs have here ok
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
			USA_clamp_bill_support = yes
		}

	}

		name = glenn.56.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 65 }

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_decrease_heartland_popularity
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_increase_southern_popularity_west
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { USA_RD_D_bill_support_new = -0.15 } #Reassured by your decision to limit the scope of this thing
			every_owned_state = { #Couple of Republicans defect to NPP-C
				limit = {

						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.5 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}

country_event = { #Bill passed
	id = glenn.58
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event glenn.58" }
	title = glenn.58.t
	desc = glenn.58.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress_2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Yay you did it champ
		name = glenn.58.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		if = { #Depending on how radical the bill was we'll have different effects
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_GLN_8_hour_workday }
			TNO_worsen_political_parties_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
			set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = -2 }
			econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = GLN_public_support_up_big
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_increase_heartland_popularity
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_decrease_southern_popularity_west
			tno_max_workhours_improve = yes
			divide_variable = { tno_max_workhours_effectiveness = 2 }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { USA_GLN_Public_Support = 6 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = USA_GLN_Public_Support
					min = 0
					max = 100
				}
				every_owned_state = { #The North rejoices
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
					}
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.12 } #Total +.17 popularity from this path
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.6 }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					US_underdog_RD_5_5 = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = { #The Midwest becomes a bit more conservative
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
					}
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.12 } #Total +.17 popularity from this path

					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.75 }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus } #Some Republicans become Democrats. Its assumed that the influx of former NPP-C will be enough to prevent Republican popularity from falling as result

				}
				every_owned_state = { #South and the Rookies are not happy
					limit = {

						NOT = { #Hit all other cultures
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
								check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							}
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.12 }
					if = { #Popularity hit is lessened at the West coast
						limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 87 } }
						subtract_from_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
					add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.75 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { #Bill was not radical
			custom_effect_tooltip = GLN_public_support_up

						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.07 } #Total +.12 popularity from this path
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.75 }

							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific

					}
				}

			}
			set_variable = { USA_C_NPP_bill_support_new = 0.15 } #Okay this thing is shaping up to be pretty damned respectable.
			set_variable = { USA_RD_R_bill_support_new = 0.10 } #Nice one pres but some of our more pro bussiness members are balking at the costs of everything
			set_variable = { USA_FR_NPP_bill_support_new = -0.15 } #Money doesn't grown on trees you know
			set_variable = { USA_RD_D_bill_support_new = -0.2 } #Glenn plz our budget is crying
			every_owned_state = { #North and rustbelt looks approvingly at you, couple of NPP-C voters defect
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				if = { #Midwest becomes less progressive
					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 85 } }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_RD_2_2 = yes
			}
			every_owned_state = { #South and Rookies look at the budget and cry
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = { #Hit all other cultures
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
			every_owned_state = { #They were afraid you'd make this thing super radical and you did
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				if = { #Another check for how radical the bill is. Redundant? Yes. Reduces code bloat? Also yes
					limit = { USA = { has_country_flag = USA_GLN_max_unemployment_benefits } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = -1 } #Convert the increase into a decrease
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
			USA_clamp_bill_support = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #I'd rather not
		name = glenn.61.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_increase_bill_support_RD_D
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_bill_support_RD_R
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_bill_support_NPP_C

			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_GLN_max_unemployment_benefits }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_decrease_heartland_popularity
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_increase_southern_popularity_west
		}
		else = { #West is not happy with you doing the bare minimum
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_decrease_heartland_popularity_west
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_increase_southern_popularity
		}
		hidden_effect = {

			set_variable = { USA_C_NPP_bill_support_new = -0.1 } #The bill is still good but this is quite the bummer
			set_variable = { USA_RD_R_bill_support_new = -0.05 } #Some of the more progressive members have their worst fears confirmed

				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee

					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }

					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 85 } }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_RD_2_2 = yes
			}
			every_owned_state = { #South and Rookies of the country slightly approves and the Democrats make gains
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }

				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }

				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_RD_2_2 = yes

				limit = {

					check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
				}

				if = { #Another check for how radical the bill is. Redundant? Yes. Reduces code bloat? Also yes
					limit = { NOT = { USA = { has_country_flag = USA_GLN_max_unemployment_benefits } } }

country_event = { #Check whether the bill passed or not
	id = glenn.62
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event glenn.62"
		#Check for bill passage
		check_if_bill_passed = yes
		if = { #Fire apropriate event depending on whether the bill passed or not
			limit = { has_country_flag = bill_passed }
			country_event = {
				id = glenn.63
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else = { #Fire apropriate event depending on whether the bill passed or not
			country_event = {
				id = glenn.64
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_bill_clear = yes
		}
	}
	title = glenn.62.t
	desc = glenn.62.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_congress3

	hidden = yes #Player should never see this
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
}

					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 } #People go to the other party
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }

							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						}

				}

					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.01 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 1 }
			if = { #If unity is below average the Democrats will raise some protests
				limit = { check_variable = { USA_RD_Unity < 15 } }
				country_event = {
					id = glenn.66
					days = 15
				}
			}

		}

	}
	option = { #
		name = glenn.65.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_GLN_increase_influence_democrats
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_add_RD_unity
		TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_low = yes
		hidden_effect = { #Increase some unity (because Glenn has been doing stuff against the democrats agenda and they like the bone
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				if = { #This has more of an effect in the non northern parts
					limit = {

							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 82 }
								check_variable = { nationality = 85 }
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.01 }
				}
				else = { #Less effective elsewhere
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.01 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
		}

				}

					}
				}

				subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }

				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }

country_event = { #Trial begins
	id = glenn.96
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event glenn.96" }
	title = glenn.96.t
	desc = glenn.96.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Let us hope for a favorable ruling
		name = glenn.96.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		if = { #Glenn favorable case
			limit = { has_country_flag = GLN_easy_case }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = { #I'll be honest I don't completely understand these triggers so this might be overkill
						USA_has_liberal_supreme_court = yes
						USA_has_very_liberal_supreme_court = yes
						USA_has_conservative_supreme_court = yes
						NOT = { USA_has_very_conservative_supreme_court = yes }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = glenn.97 days = 21 }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = glenn.98 days = 21 } } #Glenn defeated
		}
		else_if = { #Glenn bad case
			limit = { has_country_flag = GLN_bad_case }
			if = {
				limit = { USA_has_very_liberal_supreme_court = yes }
				country_event = { id = glenn.97 days = 21 }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = glenn.98 days = 21 } } #Glenn defeated
		}
		else = { #Glenn neutral case
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						USA_has_liberal_supreme_court = yes
						USA_has_very_liberal_supreme_court = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = glenn.97 days = 21 }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = glenn.98 days = 21 } } #Glenn defeated
		}
	}
}

				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }

		}
		else = { set_temp_variable = { tension_superpower_2 = JAP } }

				limit = { #WW3 is not gonna start
					check_variable = { global.TNO_superpower_tension^0 < 100 }
					check_variable = { global.TNO_superpower_tension^1 < 100 }
					check_variable = { global.TNO_superpower_tension^2 < 100 }
				}
				every_country = { country_event = { id = WORLD.782 days = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = glenn.113 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

			subtract_from_variable = { USA_GLN_Public_Support = 7 }
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_GLN_Public_Support = GLN_consequence_severity }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = USA_GLN_Public_Support
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
			divide_variable = { GLN_consequence_severity = 100 }
			every_owned_state = { #Smaller loses among core supporters
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes

						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steelbelt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.18 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = GLN_consequence_severity }
				if = { #Smaller loses in New England
					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 82 } }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.06 }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.06 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				US_underdog_NPP_5_5 = yes
			}
			every_owned_state = { #Bigger loses elsewhere
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steelbelt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.21 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = GLN_consequence_severity }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.06 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }

			var = USA_GLN_Public_Support
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_GLN_mistrusted_gov_4 days = 365 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 }
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.025 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.025 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.025 }
				US_underdog_NPP_2_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #germany reviews terms of conversion

	title = glenn.nuclear.112.t
	desc = glenn.nuclear.112.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Alles ist in Ordnung
		name = glenn.nuclear.112.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				USA = {
					set_temp_variable = {glenn_number_convertet_for_ger = 1}
					multiply_temp_variable = {glenn_number_convertet_for_ger = glenn_number_of_icbms_converted}
					divide_temp_variable = {glenn_number_convertet_for_ger = glenn_ratio_of_icbms_converted}
					check_variable = {
						var = glenn_number_convertet_for_ger
						value = 100
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = glenn.nuclear.113
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Nein nein nein das ist nicht gut
		name = glenn.nuclear.112.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				USA = {
					set_temp_variable = {glenn_number_convertet_for_ger = 1}
					multiply_temp_variable = {glenn_number_convertet_for_ger = glenn_number_of_icbms_converted}
					divide_temp_variable = {glenn_number_convertet_for_ger = glenn_ratio_of_icbms_converted}
					check_variable = {
						var = glenn_number_convertet_for_ger
						value = 100
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = glenn.nuclear.113
				}
			}
			USA = {
				country_event = {
					id = glenn.nuclear.114
					days = 5
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_conversion_germany_complained
		}
	}
}

	title = glenn.nuclear.114.t
	desc = glenn.nuclear.114.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_iberia_big_meeting

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { glenn_number_of_icbms_converted = 100 }
	}

	option = { #ok
		name = glenn.nuclear.114.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {glenn_disarmament = glenn_number_of_icbms_converted}
			divide_temp_variable = {glenn_disarmament = glenn_ratio_of_icbms_converted}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = glenn_disarmament
						value = 75
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				USA = {
					set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1 }
				}
				GER = {
					set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1 }
				}
				JAP = {
					set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				USA = {
					set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1.5 }
				}
				GER = {
					set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1.5 }
				}
				JAP = {
					set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1.5 }
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = glenn.nuclear.115
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_sabotage }
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = glenn.nuclear.115
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_sabotage }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_Glenn_nuclear_ec_conversion
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_buff }
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_disarmament }
		GER = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_disarmament } }
		JAP = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_disarmament } }
	}
}

country_event = { #agreement event for japan
	id = glenn.nuclear.122

	title = glenn.nuclear.122.t

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_japan_agrees
				}
				30 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_to_number
								has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_to_1000
							}
						}
						set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_japan_agrees
					}
				}
				25 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_to_number
								has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_to_1000
							}
						}
						set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_japan_agrees
					}
				}
				5 = {
					add_political_power = 1 #nothing
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #interesting
		name = glenn.nuclear.122.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = glenn.nuclear.123
					days = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

						has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_to_1000
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_can_be_converted
						has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_to_1000
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1.5 }
			}
			else =  {
				set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1 }
			}
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_buff }
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_disarmament }
	}
	option = { #
		name = glenn.nuclear.124.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = USA
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {

						has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_to_1000
					}
				}

			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_can_be_converted
						has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_reduce_to_1000
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1.5 }
			}
			else =  {
				set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1 }
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_sabotage }
		}
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_disarmament }
	}

	title = glenn.nuclear.207.t
	desc = glenn.nuclear.207.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_congress2

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_disarmament_germany_full
		has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_disarmament_japan_full
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_disarmament_germany_compromise
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_disarmament_japan_compromise
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_disarmament_falling_apart
		}
		tag = USA
	}

	option = { #the human race is safe for now
		name = glenn.nuclear.207.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { tension_WT = -15 }
		set_temp_variable = { tension_superpower_1 = GER }
		set_temp_variable = { tension_superpower_2 = USA }
		set_temp_variable = { tension_ID = 32 }
		TNO_change_tension = yes
		set_temp_variable = { tension_WT = -15 }
		set_temp_variable = { tension_superpower_1 = JAP }
		set_temp_variable = { tension_superpower_2 = USA }
		set_temp_variable = { tension_ID = 32 }
		TNO_change_tension = yes
		JAP = {
			country_event = glenn.nuclear.208
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = glenn.nuclear.208
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#country_event = {
			#	id = glenn.nuclear.220
			#	days = 20
			#}
			USA = {
				set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_disarmament_continue_disarm_path
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_buff }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_disarmament }
			}
			USA = {
				set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1 }
				set_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 500 }
				calculate_strike_capability = yes
			}
			GER = {
				set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1 }
				set_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 500 }
				hidden_effect = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_sabotage } }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_disarmament }
				calculate_strike_capability = yes
			}
			JAP = {
				set_variable = { GLN_nuclear_disarmament_var = -1 }
				set_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 500 }
				hidden_effect = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_sabotage } }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nuclear_disarmament }
				calculate_strike_capability = yes
			}
			BRG = {
				country_event = {
					id = glenn.nuclear.300
					days = 10
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_Glenn_nuclear_ec_pop_reduce_stockpile
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #agree
		name = glenn.nuclear.228.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GER
				}
				USA = {
					set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_ger_agrees
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = JAP
				}
				USA = {
					set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_jap_agrees
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #agree but demand to scrap the warheads
		name = glenn.nuclear.228.b
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_country_flag = usa_nuclear_keep_warheads
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GER
				}
				USA = {
					set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_ger_agrees
					clr_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_no_complaints
					country_event = {
						id = glenn.nuclear.226
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = JAP
				}
				USA = {
					set_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_jap_agrees
					clr_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_no_complaints
					country_event = {
						id = glenn.nuclear.227
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #slbm deal went through
	id = glenn.nuclear.231
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event glenn.nuclear.231" }
	title = glenn.nuclear.231.t
	desc = glenn.nuclear.231.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_jap_agrees
		has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_ger_agrees
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #weeee
		name = glenn.nuclear.231.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		GER = {
			country_event = glenn.nuclear.232
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = glenn.nuclear.232
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = glenn_nuclear_slbm_no_complaints
					}
				}
				USA = {
					subtract_from_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 200 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = glenn_nuclear_231_misc_income days = 90 }
					calculate_strike_capability = yes
				}
				JAP = {
					subtract_from_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 200 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = glenn_nuclear_231_misc_income days = 90 }
					calculate_strike_capability = yes
				}
				GER = {
					subtract_from_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 200 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = glenn_nuclear_231_misc_income days = 90 }
					calculate_strike_capability = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				USA = {
					subtract_from_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 100 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = glenn_nuclear_231_misc_income days = 90 }
					calculate_strike_capability = yes
				}
				JAP = {
					subtract_from_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 100 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = glenn_nuclear_231_misc_income days = 90 }
					calculate_strike_capability = yes
				}
				GER = {
					subtract_from_variable = { nuclear_stockpile = 100 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = glenn_nuclear_231_misc_income days = 90 }
					calculate_strike_capability = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_Glenn_nuclear_ec_cost_stockpile_reduce
	}
}
